<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第一条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>为更好地维护毕业生、用人单位和学校的利益，使校园招聘规范化、制度化，根据《关于转发〈省政府办公厅关于规范毕业生就业市场的通知〉的通知》（苏教学<span lang="EN-US">[2003]1</span>号）和《教育部关于当前形势下做好普通高等学校毕业生就业工作的通知》（教学〔<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>〕<span lang="EN-US">21</span>号）文件精神，结合学校实际情况特制定本办法。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>所有校内毕业生就业招聘活动，均由学生工作处统一管理，校内其它职能部门不得擅自举办就业招聘活动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第三条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>校园招聘的界定：校园招聘是指各用人单位通过学校相关部门联系申请、发布信息，进入校园（现场招聘、信息发布、就业咨询等）挑选毕业生的招聘形式。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>学院组织校园招聘规定<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第四条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>校内各学院举办校园招聘活动流程：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）资质审核。招聘会组织单位需对用人单位资质进行审核。用人单位必须提供招聘简章、单位地址、网址、联系人、联系电话等信息，其中企业需另提供经工商部门登记的营业执照副本复印件，事业单位另提供组织机构代码。严禁不具备法人资格的单位到学校组织招聘会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）申报审批。由各学院组织的校园招聘会，学院在审核招聘单位资质后，将相关材料和申请表报送学校就业工作办公室审批。各学院组织的相近专业招聘会，由相关学院联合举办，其中一个学院牵头申报。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、规模以下招聘会（<span lang="EN-US">20</span>家以下，含<span lang="EN-US">20</span>家）须提前一周申报。规模以下招聘会由学生工作处领导审批，并报保卫处、党委校长办公室备案。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、规模以上招聘会（<span lang="EN-US">20</span>家以上）须提前一个月申报。规模以上招聘会由学生工作处领导审核后，报主管校领导审批，并报党委校长办公室、保卫处、后勤服务集团备案。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、超过<span lang="EN-US">50</span>家（含<span lang="EN-US">50</span>家）的大型校园招聘会，校内审批后报江苏省毕业生就业工作主管部门审批。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）信息发布。经审批通过的招聘会，由就业工作办公室通过网络等方式集中向学生发布。主办方也可以通过其它方式发布。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）组织实施。招聘会主办单位应精心组织，增强针对性，提高成功率，注意现场安全，做好会议服务。规模以上招聘活动开始之前，主办单位必须配合保卫处制定安全保卫工作预案，全面落实责任，招聘过程中，须与保卫处密切配合，通力合作，有效处理突发事件，确保校园招聘会安全有序稳定。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）总结反馈。主办单位在招聘会结束后的五个工作日内，以书面材料总结招聘会举办情况，报就业工作办公室统一保存备查。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第五条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>各学院要加强对毕业生的思想教育和就业指导工作，帮助毕业生树立正确的世界观、人生观、价值观和择业观，引导毕业生理智、有选择地参加招聘活动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第三章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位校园招聘规定<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第六条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位须出具单位法人资格证明、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; "><font face="Times New Roman">&ldquo;</font></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">营业执照</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; "><font face="Times New Roman">&rdquo;</font></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">或</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; "><font face="Times New Roman">&ldquo;</font></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">注册证</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; "><font face="Times New Roman">&rdquo;</font></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">等证明材料，特殊行业（如医药卫生等）的须出具相关许可证明；中介服务机构须出具有关证明及用人单位的委托书；招聘人员须出具介绍信和身份证件。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第七条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位应将举办招聘活动的内容、方式、负责人、联系电话等与学校主办单位协商，并服从学校的统一安排。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第八条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位应遵守公开、公平、公正、自愿的原则，如实公布拟招聘的岗位、数量、条件、待遇等相关信息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第九条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位在招聘活动中张贴标语、横幅和宣传广告品等宣传材料，须经学校主办单位同意。未经同意的，不得擅自张贴，在招聘活动中不得做虚假宣传。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>用人单位在招聘活动中不得干扰、诋毁其他用人单位的招聘活动和声誉或扰乱招聘秩序，不得采取不正当竞争手段招聘毕业生，不得采用诱骗、欺诈、强行和要挟的方式与毕业生签订就业协议书；不得以招聘保密为由，进行秘密面试活动。用人单位在面试过程中应尊重毕业生的人格，保护其隐私权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十一条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>来校招聘的单位不得以任何名义向毕业生收取费用，不得要求应聘人员以其财产、证件作抵押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第四章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>毕业生参加校园招聘规定<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十二条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>毕业生参加校园招聘须服从工作人员的安排，在招聘活动中应尊重用人单位的招聘人员，不得在招聘现场大声喧哗，无理取闹，扰乱招聘秩序。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十三条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>没有落实就业单位的毕业生要积极参加学校组织的校园招聘会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十四条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>毕业生与用人单位经双向选择达成就业协议的，应签订就业协议书。协议书一经签订，对当事双方都有约束力，任何一方擅自违约都应承担相应责任。已落实单位或通过用人单位面试等已进入签约流程的毕业生原则上不应再参加其他招聘活动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十五条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>毕业生在签订协议前要如实向用人单位介绍个人情况，因弄虚作假被用人单位退回者，责任自负。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第五章　附则</span></b><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十六条　本办法适用于学校各单位组织的校园招聘活动。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十七条　本办法自公布之日起施行，由学生工作处负责解释。学校原有的相关规定与此不一致的以此为准。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 240pt; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 240pt; text-align: right; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">二○<st1:chsdate w:st="on" isrocdate="False" islunardate="False" day="16" month="9" year="2011">一一年九月十六</st1:chsdate></span></p>','False','0','0','0','2011-11-19','','0','4','0','','False')

<div align="center" style="text-align: center; line-height: 30pt; margin-top: 6pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 12pt; margin-left: 0cm; vertical-align: baseline; ">（<span>2009年6月）</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">为切实做好我省高校毕业生应征入伍学费补偿工作，根据《财政部、教育部和总参谋部关于印发〈应征入伍服义务兵役高等学校毕业生学费补偿国家助学贷款代偿暂行办法〉的通知》（财教<span style="font-size: 14pt; ">〔</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">2009</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">〕</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">35</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">号</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">）精神，结合江苏省学生资助管理信息系统实际，现将有关操作流程具体规定如下：</span></span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">一、符合规定的应征入伍毕业生学费补偿总额根据财教〔</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">2009</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">〕</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">35</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">号第五、六条确定，资金划拨统一采用&ldquo;存入毕业生个人银行账户&rdquo;方式。获得国家助学贷款的毕业生应首先将学费补偿资金用于偿还助学贷款本息。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">二、每年</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">6</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">月</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">15</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">日前，高校院系组织被确定为预征对象的毕业生填写学费补偿申请信息采集表（附件</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">1</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">），按要求签字盖章后报送校学生资助管理中心。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">三、每年</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">6</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">月</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">30</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">日前，高校学生资助管理中心会同校财务部门对预征对象的学费和国家助学贷款情况进行审核确认后，将采集表内容录入江苏省学生资助管理信息系统，集中打印学费补偿申请表（附件</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">2</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">）、办理有关签字盖章手续</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">,</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">并将预征对象申请学费补偿汇总表（附件</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">3</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">）报送省学生资助管理中心。学费补偿申请表一式两份，一份由高校留存备查，另一份交给学生。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">四、每年</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">10</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">月</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">31</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">日前，毕业生到原户籍所在地县级人民政府征兵办应征时，应当提交学费补偿申请表。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">五、对被批准入伍的应届高校毕业生，县级人民政府征兵办应在其学费补偿申请表中填写入伍批准书号和入伍通知书号，并签字盖章；每年</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">12</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">月</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">31</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">日前，将学费补偿申请表（附《应征入伍通知书》复印件）集中交送同级教育行政部门学生资助管理中心。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">六、次年元月</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">15</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">日前，县级学生资助管理中心集中审核应征入伍应届高校毕业生学费补偿材料，将审核通过的学费补偿申请书原件（含附件）寄送相应高校学生资助管理中心。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">七、我省高校在收到上述材料后</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">10</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">个工作日内，在管理系统中登记毕业生应征入伍信息，将本校应征入伍毕业生申请学费补偿汇总报表（附件</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">4</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">）连同经县级学生资助管理中心审核的学费补偿申请表原件（含附件）集中报送省学生资助管理中心。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">八、省学生资助管理中心按流程申请高校毕业生应征入伍学费补偿专项资金。中央财政将学费补偿资金下达我省后，省财政厅会同省教育厅拨付有关高校，高校根据最终审核确定的学费补偿名单和金额划拨给应征入伍毕业生。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">九、凡因财教〔</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">2009</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">〕</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">35</span><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">号第十条规定应当退还学费补偿资金的，毕业生应当主动与县级学生资助管理中心联系办理退还手续，县级学生资助管理中心应及时上缴该资金。</span></div>
<div style="text-indent: 32pt; vertical-align: baseline; "><span style="font-size: 14pt; ">十、为做好应征入伍毕业生学费补偿的服务工作，我省高校应将本操作流程复印后交给每一位预征对象。</span></div>

<div id="contents" style="padding-top: 10px; ">
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; text-align: center; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第一章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>总<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>则<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span><strong>第一条</strong><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">为了全面贯彻党的教育方针，鼓励学生争先创优、发展特长、求实创新，引导学生在知识、能力、素质诸方面协调发展，培养适应社会主义现代化建设要求的具有创新精神和实践能力的高素质人才，根据上级有关规定，结合我校实际，特制定本办法。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生素质综合测评是对学生在校期间各方面表现的测定和评价。设定的测评指标既是评价学生的基本依据，又是学生发展的导向目标。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第三条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生素质综合测评应坚持公平、公正、公开的原则，采取定量测评与定性评价相结合、过程测评与结果评价相结合、记实测评与民主评议相结合的方法，尽可能科学合理地反映学生的实际素质状况。学生素质综合测评工作每学年开展一次，在每年的<span lang="EN-US">9-10</span>月进行，毕业班在毕业前开展最后一学年的综合测评工作。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第四条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生素质综合测评的内容主要包括基本素质、课程学习成绩、实践与创新能力、奖励与惩处四部分，测评结果＝基本分＋奖励加分－惩处扣分，基本分按百分制计算，其中基本素质占<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分，课程学习成绩占<span lang="EN-US">60</span>分，实践与创新能力占<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第五条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">本办法适用于本校正式注册的普通本科学生。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>基本素质测评<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: larger; "><strong>第六条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></strong>基本素质是指学生在思想道德修养、人生规划、学习态度、科学人文修养、身心健康等方面应当具有的符合时代特征的基本品质，是学生世界观、人生观、价值观、道德观及其行为表现等方面的综合体现。</span><span><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第七条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">基本素质测评的基本内容及其基本要求：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）思想道德修养。主要考察政治态度、法纪观念、集体观念、道德品质以及生活态度。基本要求：拥护党的路线、方针和政策，坚持正确的政治方向，热爱社会主义祖国，关心时事，自觉加强政治修养，认真上好思想政治理论课和形式政策教育课等，积极参加各项政治学习和活动；自觉遵守国家法律、法规和学校的各项规章制度，无违法违纪行为；顾全大局，有团结协作精神，积极参加各项集体活动，维护集体荣誉；自觉遵守公共秩序和社会公德，诚实守信，为人正直，敬老爱幼，尊敬师长，团结同学，乐于助人；发扬艰苦奋斗精神，生活俭朴，不浪费粮食，节约水、电，不向学校和家庭提出超越实际可能的生活要求。对有见义勇为、舍己救人、扶残助弱、拾金不昧、无偿献血等事迹者（有经认定的事迹材料或书面证明），可评定为优。对有违反宪法所确定的基本原则的言行并坚持不改者；违反国家法律、法规或校纪校规受到处分者；有严重损害集体和他人利益的行为者；不讲社会公德，不讲诚信，言谈举止粗俗，品行不端者或一贯生活铺张浪费者，应评定为差。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）人生规划。主要考察大学生涯设计和职业生涯规划情况。基本要求：以就业为核心，以&ldquo;考研、出国、技能培养&rdquo;为导向，制定有明确的大学目标规划并付诸实施，能根据自身的发展情况及时调整和完善规划；对自己的职业发展方向有合理的定位。对没有制定大学目标规划或光有规划但不付诸实施者，应评定为差。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）学习态度。主要考察平时对待课程学习的态度和学风。基本要求：学习态度端正，遵守学习纪律，谦虚好学，刻苦认真，在努力完成各项学习任务中树立良好学风。对学习不求上进，违反学习纪律，经常旷课或迟到早退，不按时完成作业或弄虚作假者，应评定为差。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）科学人文修养。主要考察科学态度、文化艺术修养和审美情趣。基本要求：有科学的思想方法，了解文学、历史、哲学、艺术和自然科学等方面的基本常识，有较强的口头和文字表达能力以及审美能力，有高雅的生活情趣和高尚的精神追求。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）身心健康。主要考察参加体育锻炼情况、生活适应能力和在面临困难、挫折时的心理表现及心理调适能力。基本要求：认真上好体育课，积极参加早操、课外体育锻炼和体育竞赛活动，有健康的体魄，体质测试成绩合格；积极掌握心理卫生的基本知识，建立良好的人际关系，努力增强挫折耐受力、情绪控制力和社会适应力。对体质测试成绩不合格者，应评定为差。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第八条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">基本素质测评在学院领导下，针对学生参加的教育环节、课外活动、日常表现、素质状况等实际情况，采取民主评议、班主任考核和辅导员考核相结合的方法，根据基本素质测评的五个方面，分项进行评分，各项之和即为基本素质测评分（<span lang="EN-US">G1</span>，满分为<span lang="EN-US">30</span>分），其计算公式：<span lang="EN-US">G1=G</span><span>&prime;</span>&times;<span lang="EN-US">30%+G</span><span>&prime;&prime;</span>&times;<span lang="EN-US">40%+ G</span><span>&prime;&prime;&prime;</span>&times;<span lang="EN-US">30%<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">民主评议采取逐人分项进行，全班民主评议得分总和平均值为<span lang="EN-US">G</span><span>&prime;</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">班主任、辅导员根据学生一学年的综合表现评分，其评分结果分别为<span lang="EN-US">G</span><span>&prime;&prime;</span>、<span lang="EN-US">G</span><span>&prime;&prime;&prime;</span>。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第三章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>课程学习成绩测评<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span><strong>第九条</strong><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">课程学习成绩是指学生所修专业教学计划规定课程的考核成绩（非百分制成绩折算成百分制），若课程成绩评定为优、良、中、及格和不及格的，则分别换算为<span lang="EN-US">95</span>、<span lang="EN-US">85</span>、<span lang="EN-US">75</span>、<span lang="EN-US">65</span>和<span lang="EN-US">50</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">课程学习成绩测评分（<span lang="EN-US">G2</span>）由班主任或班主任带领班干部进行计算，满分<span lang="EN-US">60</span>分。课程学习成绩测评分（<span lang="EN-US">G2</span>）＝（必修课程平均学分成绩＋选修课程折算成绩）&times;<span lang="EN-US">60%</span>，其中，选修课程折算成绩计算办法为：每通过一门加<span lang="EN-US">0.005</span>&times;该门课程的考核成绩。<span lang="EN-US" style="background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: rgb(217, 217, 217); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第四章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>实践与创新能力测评<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span><strong>第十一条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></strong>实践与创新能力是指学生在学习、工作、科技和社会活动中所表现出的创新素养以及运用所掌握的知识分析和解决实际问题的能力，主要考察本学年度内学生在科技学术、社会工作、文学艺术、文体竞赛以及其他实践活动等方面获得的成果。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十二条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">实践与创新能力测评分（<span lang="EN-US">G3</span>）由基本分和成果分两部分组成，满分<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十三条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">基本分（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>分）主要考察学生的创新意识以及学生参加社会工作、社会实践活动的总体表现，由学生民主评议分（占<span lang="EN-US">30</span>％）、班主任测评分（占<span lang="EN-US">40</span>％）和辅导员测评分（占<span lang="EN-US">30</span>％）三部分组成。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 16px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 25px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十四条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 25px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">成果分（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>分）主要考察学生在学科与文体竞赛、科技发明、科研成果、社会活动、考证考级等方面取得的成绩，由辅导员负责评分。评分标准如下：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 16px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 25px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）<span lang="EN-US">3</span>－<span lang="EN-US">5</span>分<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学科竞赛或文体竞赛：获得校级特等奖、一等奖或第一名，在市级及以上竞赛中获得名次；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在省级及以上刊物（含全国性报纸）发表论文或文章或公开出版学术、文学、艺术等著作；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">获得省级及以上先进个人称号或撰写的调查报告、实践报告获得省级及以上奖项；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">非计算机专业学生通过计算机四级考试、计算机专业学生通过计算机专业高级考试。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）<span lang="EN-US">2</span>－<span lang="EN-US">3</span>分<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在校级学科竞赛或文体竞赛中获得特等奖、一等奖或第一名以外的名次；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">获得校级及以上先进个人称号或撰写的调查报告、实践报告获得校级及以上奖项；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在校级刊物（含校报）发表文章；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">非英语专业学生通过<span lang="EN-US">CET-6</span>考试、英语专业学生通过专业英语八级考试、日语专业学生通过国家一级考试、非计算机专业学生通过计算机三级考试、计算机专业学生通过计算机专业中级考试。通过出国留学水平测试（雅思、托福等）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）<span lang="EN-US">0</span>－<span lang="EN-US">2</span>分<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在院级学科竞赛或文体竞赛中获得名次；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">获得院级先进个人称号或撰写的调查报告、实践报告获得院级奖项；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.&nbsp;</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在院级刊物（含院报）发表文章；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">非英语专业学生通过<span lang="EN-US">CET-4</span>考试、英语专业学生通过专业英语四级考试、日语专业学生通过国家二级考试、非计算机专业学生通过计算机国家或省级二级考试、计算机专业学生通过专业计算机国家初级考试。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">获得其他与就业有关的证书。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十五条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在实践与创新能力测评中弄虚作假、虚报成果的，经核实后扣除所获得的评分，并将其基本素质测评总评得分记为零分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第五章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>奖励与惩处<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span><strong>第十六条</strong><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">奖励加分（<span lang="EN-US">A<sub>1</sub></span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）学生党支部、班集体、团支部等集体取得突出成绩受到学院及以上组织表彰并授予荣誉称号的，对其所有成员予以加分（具体标准见表二），但因同一原因获得不同的荣誉称号或表彰的，只计最高分，不累计加分，每人奖励加分最高不超过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">表二：先进集体成员加分<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）所在宿舍被评为校级文明宿舍的，宿舍成员每人加<span lang="EN-US">0.5</span>分；被评为院级文明宿舍的，宿舍成员每人加<span lang="EN-US">0.2</span>分。同时被评为校级文明宿舍和院级文明宿舍的，宿舍成员每人加<span lang="EN-US">0.5</span>分。<span lang="EN-US" style="background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: rgb(217, 217, 217); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 28pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十七条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">惩处扣分（<span lang="EN-US">A<sub>2</sub></span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）无故旷课、旷操者每次扣<span lang="EN-GB">0.2</span>分；<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）在校期间未请假夜不归宿者每次扣<span lang="EN-GB">0.5</span>分；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）对综合测评态度不端正者扣<span lang="EN-GB">1</span>分，无故不参加综合测评者扣<span lang="EN-GB">2</span>分；<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）违反校纪校规受警告处分者扣<span lang="EN-GB">2</span>分，受严重警告处分者扣<span lang="EN-GB">2.5</span>分，受记过处分者扣<span lang="EN-GB">3</span>分，受留校察看处分者扣<span lang="EN-GB">3.5</span>分；<span lang="EN-GB"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 22pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）因同一原因扣分的，只计最高分，不累计扣分。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第六章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>测评结果及其应用<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span><strong>第十八条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></strong>每学年学生素质综合测评的最终结果（<span lang="EN-US">G</span>）由班主任或班主任带领班干部进行计算，其计算公式为：<span lang="EN-US">G=G1+G2+G3</span>＋<span lang="EN-US">A<sub>1</sub></span>－<span lang="EN-US">A<sub>2<o:p></o:p></sub></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十九条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">测评结果经学院审核后，在本测评单位内公布。若有异议，应由学院核查后作出裁决。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">测评结果体现学生综合素质的相对水平，作为下列各项工作的依据：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）评定各类奖学金的基本依据；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）评选三好学生、三好学生标兵、优秀学生干部、优秀毕业生等先进个人荣誉称号的基本依据；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）评选先进班集体等先进集体荣誉称号的基本依据之一；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）审批困难补助、减免学费的申请等学生资助项目的考查依据之一；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）毕业生就业推荐、与学生家长沟通等工作的基本依据之一；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（六）推荐免试研究生的参考依据。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<h3 style="margin-top: 8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 4pt; margin-left: 0cm; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第七章<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>附<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>则<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></h3>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><span><strong>第二十一条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></strong>本办法由学生工作处负责解释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 24pt; line-height: 23pt; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十二条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">本办法自发布之日起施行，此前有关文件规定与本办法不一致的，以本办法为准。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
