<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">b.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">道德品质优良，行为举止文明，学习成绩优秀。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">c.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">遵纪守法，遵守社会公德，树立社会主义荣辱观，模范执行学校规章制度。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">d.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">积极参加公益劳动和社会实践等社会主义精神文明建设活动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">e.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">积极参加体育锻炼，达到《国家学生体质健康标准》。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">f.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">连续两次获得过院级以上&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;表彰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）省级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">a.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">具备省级&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;条件。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">b.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">担任班级、党团支部和校、院学生会主要干部，热心社会工作，热情为同学服务。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">c.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学习刻苦，严于律己，努力工作，在同学中具有较高的威信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）省级&ldquo;先进班集体&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">a.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">有政治坚定、团结协作、以身作则、联系群众的班委会。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">b.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">有积极上进、团结互助、遵纪守法、崇尚科学、热爱集体、朝气蓬勃、文明健康的良好班风。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">c.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">有严谨求实、刻苦钻研、奋发向上的优良学风。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">d.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">积极参与校风建设和争做文明先锋活动。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">e.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">保持良好的宿舍卫生环境和个人卫生习惯。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">f.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">全班同学都达到《国家学生体质健康标准》</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">g.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">上一年度获得校级先进集体表彰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">评比程序及要求<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）学校在收到省教育厅、团省委《关于评选普通高校省级三好学生优秀学生干部和先进班集体的通知》后，将名额分配到各学院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）各学院根据分配名额，对照评比条件，在全院范围内推荐，并将推荐名单在全院范围内公示，公示无异议后，将推荐名单和相关材料报</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生工作处</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">，逾期不报视为弃权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）学校组织评审，根据评比条件和指标</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">审核确定名单并报分管校领导审批，名单在全校范围内公示后，上报省教育厅审批。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）其它省级学生先进个人和先进集体评比办法参照上级有关文件执行。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">二、校级&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;、&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;、&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;、&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;和&ldquo;先进班集体&rdquo;评比<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）评比对象<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">本校正式注册的普通本科学生个人和班集体。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）评比条件<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）能够认真学习邓小平理论、&ldquo;三个代表&rdquo;重要思想和科学发展观，具有坚定正确的政治方向、良好的道德品质、模范执行学校的规章制度。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）当学年综合测评位列同一年级同一专业排名的前<span lang="EN-US">50</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）学习刻苦，学习成绩优良，当学年获得国家奖学金、国家励志奖学金或学校奖学金。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">4</span>）积极参加体育锻炼和各项课外活动，达到《国家学生体质健康标准》。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）具备校级&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;条件。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）当学年获得国家奖学金、国家励志奖学金或校长奖学金。<s><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></s></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）校、院级学生组织干部，班级、党团支部干部。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）能够认真学习邓小平理论、&ldquo;三个代表&rdquo;重要思想和科学发展观，具有坚定正确的政治方向、良好的道德品质、模范执行学校的规章制度。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）工作积极，热心为同学服务，对所承担的工作认真负责，有创新精神，工作效率较高，工作成绩突出，当学年工作考核结果为&ldquo;优秀&rdquo;。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">4</span>）当学年综合测评位列同一年级同一专业排名的前<span lang="EN-US">50</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>）学习刻苦，学习成绩良好，当学年必修课成绩全部及格及以上。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>）积极参加体育锻炼和各项课外活动，达到《国家学生体质健康标准》。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）应届毕业生。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）政治表现和思想品德优良，历年均获得校级或院级&ldquo;</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">三好学生标兵&rdquo;、&ldquo;</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">三好学生&rdquo;或&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;表彰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）积极参加体育锻炼和各项课外活动，达到《国家学生体质健康标准》。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">4</span>）<span>凡</span>毕业前<span>有下列情况之一者，取消其&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;称号：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">a.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国家法律、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">校纪校规受到学校处分</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">b.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">不能获得学士学位。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;先进班集体&rdquo;<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>）全班同学能认真学习邓小平理论和&ldquo;三个代表&rdquo;重要思想和形势政策；政治觉悟高，积极要求进步；诚实守信，自觉遵守校纪校规，有较高的道德水平和文明修养，当学年班级无人受各种纪律处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>）全班同学都制定有明确的大学目标规划，学习目的明确，学习态度端正，上课认真听讲，出勤率高，不迟到，不早退，认真完成作业。学习风气浓厚，学习成绩优良，当学年全班课程学分加权平均成绩名列本年级本专业前茅。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">3</span>）班委、团支部团结合作、工作能力强，威信高，能按时完成上级组织安排的工作；班团干部能以身作则，班级工作公正、公平、透明度高；班级内部团结友爱、互帮互助，凝聚力强。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">4</span>）全班同学自觉遵守宿舍管理规定；宿舍布置整洁、文明、高雅，学习氛围浓厚，积极创建文明宿舍。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>）积极开展健康向上的校园科技、文化、体育活动；积极参加校、院两级各项活动并取得突出成绩；全班<span lang="EN-US">95%</span>的同学达到《国家学生体质健康标准》</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）评比程序及要求<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级先进个人和先进集体由各学院根据评比条件和指标负责评比、公示，公示无异议后，学院在规定时间前将有关材料报学生工作处，学生工作处审核后报分管校领导批准、发文。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;和&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;不可兼评。校级&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;评比比例不超过参评学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>％；校级&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;评比比例不超过参评学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>％；校级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;评比比例不超过参评学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>％；被评为校级&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;或&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;，同时符合校级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;条件的，可以同时评为校级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;，不占校级&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;比例；校级&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;评比比例不超过参评学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>％；校级&ldquo;先进班集体&rdquo;评比比例不超过全校参评班级数的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><br />
</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 宋体; ">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、校级先进个人和先进集体评比工作每学年开展一次，其中校级&ldquo;三好学生&rdquo;、&ldquo;三好学生标兵&rdquo;和&ldquo;优秀学生干部&rdquo;评比工作结合学生学年小结，在每年的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月中旬开展。&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;评比工作在每年的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月下旬开展。毕业班最后一学年的先进个人和先进班集体评比工作与毕业鉴定同时进行。<span lang="EN-US"><br />
<span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span>三、校级单项奖评比<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">五四表彰类：优秀团员、优秀团干、五四红旗团支部、五四青年奖章，根据《南京信息工程大学五四表彰评比办法》进行评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）社会实践类：先进个人、优秀调查报告、优秀团队、先进单位，根据《南京信息工程大学社会实践评优办法》进行评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）学生组织类：优秀团学组织学生干部、优秀社团干部、十佳社团，根据《南京信息工程大学优秀团学组织学生干部评比办法》、《南京信息工程大学优秀社团干部评比办法》、《南京信息工程大学十佳社团评比办法》进行评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）活动项目类：优秀青年志愿者、校园文化活动先进个人、创新创业先进个人，根据《南京信息工程大学优秀青年志愿者评比办法》、《南京信息工程大学校园文化活动先进个人评比办法》、《南京信息工程大学创新创业先进个人评比办法》进行评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）国防生先进个人和先进集体：</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">优秀国防生、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国防生学习标兵</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国防生遵章守纪标兵</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国防生内务卫生标兵、国防生军事训练标兵、优秀国防生干部、国防生学习进步奖、优秀毕业国防生、国防生先进模拟排、国防生先进模拟班，根据</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">《南京信息工程大学</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国防生先进个人和先进集体</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">评比办法</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">》</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">进行评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（六）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">其它各级各类单项奖的评比</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">参照各自评选办法执行。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">四、凡被评为省级或校级先进个人的学生，评比材料存入本人档案并作为毕业生就业推荐内容。&ldquo;优秀毕业生&rdquo;在就业时，依据国家的有关政策规定，结合用人单位的需求，学校给予优先推荐。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">五、本办法自发布之日起施行，此前有关文件规定与本办法不一致的，以本办法为准。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">六、各学院可参照本办法制定院级学生先进个人和先进集体评比办法。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">七、本办法由学生工作部（处）负责解释。其中，各级各类单项奖评比办法由颁布单位负责解释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="right" style="font-family: Verdana, Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif, 宋体; font-size: 14px; margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 16pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: right; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

            <div class="Section1">
            <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; ">&nbsp;</p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">为加强学生宿舍管理，提高学生文明素质，创建优良的学习、生活环境，促进学生德、智、体、美全面发展，构建和谐校园，特制定本办法。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">一、评选条件<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）文明风范<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员关心国家大事，关心学校建设发展，关心班集体的各项事务，积极参加时事政治理论学习和学校各项公益活动；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">舍成员奋发向上，团结友爱，互帮互助，有正义感和集体荣誉感，人际关系和谐；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员遵纪守法，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">严格执行各项规章制度，遵守作息时间，不擅自留宿外来人员，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">无私自在外租住、未经请假夜不归宿现象；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员尊敬师长，礼貌待人，尊重管理人员，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">服从管理人员的管理，积极配合检查人员的工作</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员遵守社会公德，爱护公共财物，爱惜粮食，节约水电；<span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;<br />
            <span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>6.</span>宿舍成员重视宿舍内精神文明建设，不张贴不健康、不文明的图片和画像；不看、不听、不传播不健康的书刊、音像、信息；积极开展健康有益的文体活动；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">7</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员安全意识强，具备基本的安全知识，发现隐患及时报告。不私接电源、乱拉网线、违章使用大功率电器。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）学习风气<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员学习目的明确，态度端正，宿舍有浓厚的学习气氛，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">无沉迷网络、学习（自修）时间在宿舍玩电脑游戏、看影碟等</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">使用计算机从事与学习无关活动等现象。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员严格遵守考试纪律，无考试违纪或考试作弊现象。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）环境卫生<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">地面整洁，无杂乱物品，无污垢；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍内家具、书架等物品摆放整齐有序；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">门、窗、纱窗无灰尘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">天棚四壁、灯管无蜘蛛网，灯管无灰尘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">门前无堆放垃圾，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">阳台干净无杂物；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">6.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">墙面整洁，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">无乱涂乱画乱张贴，无鞋印、手印、球印；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">7.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">桌面干净，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">书籍、衣物、鞋子等物品摆放整齐；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">8.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">床上卧具干净整齐划一，位置摆放得当，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">无床帘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">9.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍张贴有卫生轮值表，宿舍无异味。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">&nbsp;有下列情况之一的，不能评为文明宿舍：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">宿舍成员中有违纪受处分者；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">不服从有关部门管理和检查；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">由于人为原因造成安全事故；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">一学年内宿舍环境卫生检查结果不合格次数达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次及以上。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">二、检查与评选办法<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）学生宿舍日常检查工作由后勤总公司宿舍管理部门负责，宿舍管理人员</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">每两周至少一次对学生宿舍进行全面检查、评分和成绩公布，检查大功率电器使用、学生晚归、夜不归宿等违纪情况并记录；各学院要结合实际，采取学院检查和学生自律组织检查相结合的方式，定期对学生宿舍进行抽查。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">文明宿舍评选活动每学年评比一次，在每年的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>－<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月开展。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）符合评选条件的宿舍可向学院提出书面申请，学院根据评选办法，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">按比例进行推荐和申报。学院在推荐和申报前，首先要对</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">申报宿舍进行初审和公示，经公示无异议后，将申报名单和申报表等相关推荐材料报送学生工作处；学生宿舍管理工作领导小组进行复审，经公示无异议后，将评选结果报分管校领导签发。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）评选工作坚持&ldquo;公开、公平、公正&rdquo;原则，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">坚持标准，实事求是，宁缺毋滥。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
            <p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">三、结果使用<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
