<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二条&nbsp;</span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">处分违纪学生应做到</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">程序正当、证据充分、依据明确、定性准确、处分适当。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第三条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">纪律处分的种类分为：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）警告；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）严重警告；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）记过；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）留校察看；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）开除学籍。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第四条&nbsp;</span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;</span>有下列情形之一的，可从轻或减轻处分：<span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）违纪后主动承认违纪行为，认识深刻，悔改表现突出的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）能主动揭发他人违纪行为，经查证属实的。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第五条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">对违纪应受处分，有下列情形之一者，加重一级处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）违纪后，拒不承认错误；或提供伪证，妨碍调查处理；或受处分后借口申述，无理纠缠，态度恶劣者；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）对检举人、证人或管理人员有威胁或打击报复行为者；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）在本校已受过处分者。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第六条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反宪法，反对四项基本原则、破坏安定团结、扰乱社会秩序的，给予开除学籍处分；组织成立非法组织或未经有关部门批准擅自策划、组织大型集会、游行、示威等活动的，给予开除学籍处分；参与非法组织、集会、游行、示威等活动，视情节轻重给予批评教育或警告处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第七条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">触犯国家法律、构成刑事犯罪的，给予开除学籍处分。违反治安管理规定受到处罚，性质恶劣的，给予开除学籍处分；其他违反治安管理规定的行为，视情节轻重给予记过或留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第八条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反学校管理规定，影响学校教育教学秩序、生活秩序以及公共场所管理秩序，侵害其他个人、组织合法权益，尚未构成犯罪的，视情节和后果给予以下处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）违反学校规定，影响学校教育教学秩序、生活秩序以及公共场所管理秩序，侵害其他个人、组织合法权益的，给予警告、严重警告或记过处分。情节和后果严重的，给予留校察看或开除学籍处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）妨碍国家工作人员、学校管理人员依法或依据校纪校规执行公务的，视情节和后果轻重给予警告直至留校察看处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）故意破坏公共设施，损害学校或他人财产，违章用电、用火及使用其他危险物品，造成后果的，除赔偿经济损失外，给予严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）有性骚扰等流氓行为，酗酒滋事，赌博或提供赌博条件的，给予严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）传播、复制非法书刊或音像制品，参与非法传销或进行邪教、封建迷信活动的，给予严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（六）侮辱、诽谤、诬告、陷害或威胁他人，侵犯他人通信自由的，给予警告、严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（七）擅自在学校宿舍里留宿他人，给予警告或严重警告处分。<span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第九条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">应当在学校统一安排的宿舍居住的学生未经学校批准夜不归宿，每学期累计达到一定次数者，给予以下处理：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次，给予警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，给予严重警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次，给予记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次及以上，给予留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在外租房居住，违反有关规定，给学校带来不良影响的，给予记过或留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在人际交往中行为不当，严重违反社会公德，视情节轻重给予记过或留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十一条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">偷窃、诈骗国家、集体、个人财物，尚未构成犯罪的，视情节轻重给予下列处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）价值不满<span lang="EN-US">500</span>元者，给予警告或严重警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）价值在<span lang="EN-US">500</span>元以上<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元以内者，给予严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）价值在<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元以上者，给予记过或留校察看处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）价值虽不满<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元，但属屡教不改者也给予记过或留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十二条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">对违反国家关于计算机网络使用的有关规定，尚未构成犯罪的，视情节及危害程度分别给予以下处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）在网络上撰写或传播具有歪曲事实或侮辱诽谤他人人格、淫秽、暴力等有害信息，造成不良影响的，给予记过或留校察看处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）故意制作、传播计算机病毒等破坏性程序，破坏计算机系统正常运行的，给予严重警告或记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）通过网络盗用他人<span lang="EN-US">IP</span>地址、用户帐号，危害网络安全的，给予警告或严重警告处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十三条&nbsp;</span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;</span>组织、策划或参与打架、斗殴，尚未构成犯罪的，除承担相应的经济赔偿（含受害者的医药费、护理费、必需的营养费等费用）责任以外，分别给予以下处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）斗殴、打架的策划者、肇事者，给予记过处分；其中情节严重的，给予留校察看处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）参与打架、斗殴的，视情节轻重给予警告或严重警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）故意为他人打架提供器械的，给予记过处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十四条<span lang="EN-US"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">吸食毒品，视情节轻重给予记过或留校察看处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十五条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">一学期累计旷课达到一定学时者，给予相应处理：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）<span lang="EN-US">16</span>学时，给予警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）<span lang="EN-US">24</span>学时，给予严重警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）<span lang="EN-US">32</span>学时，给予记过处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）<span lang="EN-US">40</span>学时，给予留校察看处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）一学期累计旷课达到<span lang="EN-US">50</span>学时或未请假离校连续两周未参加规定的教学活动的，予以退学。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十六条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反考试规定的，给予以下处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）考生不遵守考场纪律，不服从考试工作人员的安排与要求，有下列考试违纪行为之一的，给予警告或严重警告处分；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">携带规定以外的物品进入考场或者未放在指定位置的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">未在规定的座位参加考试的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">考试开始信号发出前答题或者考试结束信号发出后继续答题的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在考试过程中旁窥、交头接耳、互打暗号或者手势的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">在考场或者教育考试机构禁止的范围内，喧哗、吸烟或者实施其他影响考场秩序的行为的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">6.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">未经考试工作人员同意在考试过程中擅自离开考场的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">7.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">将试卷、答卷（含答题卡、答题纸等，下同）、草稿纸等考试用纸带出考场的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">8.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">用规定以外的笔或者纸答题或者在试卷规定以外的地方书写姓名、考号或者以其他方式在答卷上标记信息的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">9.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">其他违反考场规则但尚未构成作弊的行为。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）有以下作弊行为的，给予记过处分；其中情节严重的，给予留校察看处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">携带与考试内容相关的文字材料或者存储有与考试内容相关资料的电子设备参加考试的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">抄袭或者协助他人抄袭试题答案或者与考试内容相关的资料的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">抢夺、窃取他人试卷、答卷或者强迫他人为自己抄袭提供方便的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">故意销毁试卷、答卷或者考试材料的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">传、接物品或者交换试卷、答卷、草稿纸的；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">6.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">其他作弊行为。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）有以下作弊行为的，视情节轻重，给予留校察看或开除学籍处分：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">由他人代替考试或替他人参加考试；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">组织作弊；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">使用通讯设备作弊；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">其他作弊行为严重的。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十七条&nbsp;</span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;</span>剽窃、抄袭他人研究成果的，给予记过或留校察看处分，情节严重的，给予开除学籍处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十八条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">弄虚作假，伪造证件，欺骗组织，蒙骗他人，尚未构成犯罪的，视情节轻重给予严重警告或记过处分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第十九条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生留校察看期一般为一年，从发文之日计算。对受到留校察看处分的学生，学生所在学院应当定期进行考察，及时帮助教育。在留校察看期间，如有显著悔改表现，可提前解除对其留校察看。留校察看期满者，学校应视其表现，及时作出按期解除对其留校察看或延长留校察看期的决定。到期未作出延后解除规定的，应视为自动解除。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学生受到留校察看处分且在毕业前未能解除察看，学校对其作结业处理。待其察看期满后，经本人申请，所在单位或街道办事处证明其确已改正错误，学院审核符合毕业条件的，学校可换发毕业证书。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十一条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">被开除学籍的学生，由学校发给学习证明。学生在一周内离校，档案、户口退回其家庭户籍所在地。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十二条&nbsp;<span style="color: red; "><span>&nbsp;</span></span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">本规定没有列举的违纪行为确应给予处分的，可参照最相近条款给予处分。<span lang="EN-US" style="color: red; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十三条</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">对学生的处分材料，学校真实完整地归入学校文书档案和本人档案。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">第二十四条&nbsp;<span>&nbsp;</span></span></b><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">本规定自发布之日起施行。原有规定凡与本规定不一致的，以本规定为准。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）校长奖学金：每人每学年<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>元，占学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>％左右。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）一等奖学金：每人每学年<span lang="EN-US">1000</span>元，不超过学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）二等奖学金：每人每学年<span lang="EN-US">800</span>元，不超过学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" align="left" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; text-align: left; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）三等奖学金：每人每学年<span lang="EN-US">400</span>元，不超过学生总数的<span lang="EN-US">24</span>％。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 7.8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">三、评定条件<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">参加学校奖学金评选的学生必须同时具备以下条件：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">具有坚定正确的政治方向，坚持党的基本路线，认真学习马列主义、毛泽东思想、邓小平理论和&ldquo;三个代表&rdquo;重要思想；</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">有较高思想政治素质和良好的文明行为习惯，模范遵守和执行《高等学校学生行为准则》和学校有关规章制度；<span lang="EN-US"><br />
<span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">积极参加社会实践和科技活动，善于学习和吸收新知识，有较强的实践能力和开拓创新精神；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">勤奋学习，成绩优良；<span lang="EN-US"><br />
<span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">积极参加体育锻炼和文娱活动，身心健康，体质测试成绩达到《国家学生体质健康标准》；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">6.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">评定学年综合测评成绩名列同一年级同一专业<span lang="EN-US">50%</span>之前。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">凡评定学年中有下列情况之一者，不具备评奖资格：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">1.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">未注册；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">2.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">国家法律、</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">校纪校规受到学校处分或留校</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">察看未解除</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">或</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">违反国家法律、校纪校规，正在调查处理之中；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">3.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">必修课程有不及格科目；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">4.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">平均学分绩点＜<span lang="EN-US">2.0</span>（<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年以后入学的学生，含<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>级学生）；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">5.</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">评定学年所获得学分＜<span lang="EN-US">40</span></span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学分（已修满足够学分者除外）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">。<span lang="EN-US" style="background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: rgb(217, 217, 217); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">四、评定办法及有关要求</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学校奖学金每学年评定一次，在综合测评的基础上，与国家奖学金、国家励志奖学金的评定同时进行，每年的<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">～<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月评定上一学年学校奖学金。</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">学校奖学金与国家奖学金、国家励志奖学金不可兼得。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）评定学校奖学金时，按必修课程平均学分成绩与选修课程折算成绩之和，在同一年级同一专业的排名情况，评比决定获奖学金的学生。其中，选修课程折算成绩计算方法为：每通过一门加<span lang="EN-US">0.005</span>&times;该门课程的考核成绩。<span lang="EN-US" style="background-image: initial; background-attachment: initial; background-origin: initial; background-clip: initial; background-color: rgb(217, 217, 217); background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; "><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）各学院要坚持公开、公平、公正的原则，</span><span style="font-size: 16pt; color: black; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">初评名单在上报学生工作处以前，应事先在学院公示，充分征求师生意见。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; "><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 7.8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 33.6pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">五、其它<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）评定奖学金依据的成绩以教务处认定的首次考核成绩为准，考核成绩若为非百分制则折算成百分制，若课程成绩评定为优、良、中、及格和不及格的，则分别换算为<span lang="EN-US">95</span>、<span lang="EN-US">85</span>、<span lang="EN-US">75</span>、<span lang="EN-US">65</span>和<span lang="EN-US">50</span>分。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（二）转专业的学生在评定学年所在学院参加奖学金评比。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（三）高水平运动员和部分少数民族学生的选课和成绩计算按教务处相关规定执行。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（四）毕业班在毕业前评定最后一学年的奖学金。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（五）学校对获得奖学金的学生颁发&ldquo;奖学金证书&rdquo;。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（六）学生领取的奖学金不能用于诸如请客吃饭、抽烟酗酒等，违者将追回所获奖学金和&ldquo;奖学金证书&rdquo;，同时不能参与下一学年奖学金的评定。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 7.8pt; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32.15pt; line-height: 21px; "><b><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">六、附则<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-top: 0cm; margin-right: 0cm; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0cm; padding-top: 0px; padding-right: 0px; padding-bottom: 0px; padding-left: 0px; list-style-type: none; list-style-position: initial; list-style-image: initial; text-indent: 32pt; line-height: 21px; "><span style="font-size: 16pt; line-height: 31px; font-family: 仿宋_GB2312; ">（一）本办法由学生工作处负责解释。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 电讯盈科企业方案外包开发中心运用PRINCE2、SSADM、PMP等国际最佳实践开发方法学和项目管理经验，引入成熟的应用程序开发和管理流程，并拥有ISO27001、ISO20000、ISO9001、CMMI第五级等各项国际专业认证，为客户提供综合、全面的IT解决方案以及外包服务，包括：数据中心托管、IT基础设施建设、应用程序开发和管理、ERP实施和维护、云计算服务，以及根据不同行业需求度身定制的业务流程外包服务。</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">东南融通信息科技（苏州）有限公司（外包第三名）</span></p>

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 东南融通的IT外包服务，是东南融通在专注行业领先的金融领域IT服务的基础上，在全球化的战略目标下，逐步成长和发展起来的多元化IT服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 东南融通的IT外包服务，秉承和弘扬金融IT服务领域积累的优质理念和最佳实践， 延展和丰富IT服务的范围、层次和能力，通过规模经济、地域辐射和成本优势，在全球范围内，为本土和跨国企业提供全方位的优质服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 经过数年的积累，东南融通建立了一支具有丰富外包服务和咨询实施经验的外包管理和服务团队，形成了海内外良性互动、通用服务和行业服务结合、服务模式多样化的高品质业务体系，服务团队广泛分布于大中华区、东南亚、北美和欧洲等区域，多区域的人力资源优势更是为外包服务提供了广泛的空间。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 作为一家全球性的服务外包企业，东南融通所服务的客户涵盖北美、欧洲的跨国企业，跨国企业在中国投资的公司，以及中国领先的行业企事业单位和机构。</p>

<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 新宇软件有限公司成立于2003年，是全球领先的信息技术服务供应商。新宇软件在金融、电信、高科技制造、房地产、零售及游戏等行业积累了丰富的行业经验，为客户提供企业解决方案、软件产品工程、应用软件开发和维护、质量保证和测试、离岸研发中心及业务流程外包等全方位的IT服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 为了更好的满足客户需求，为客户提供高质量的服务，新宇软件在苏州成立之后，已经相继在中国上海、广州、扬州及美国波士顿、旧金山等地设立了分支机构，全球员工2800余人，其中包括来自美国、德国、印度、俄罗斯、英国、法国、日本，西班牙、新加坡等十多个国家的优秀技术和管理人才，为客户提供优质、高效的服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 新宇软件是CMMI5级认证企业，并通过了IS09001质量管理体系、ISO27001信息安全体系认证。基于独特的全球交付模式和完善的项目管理流程，新宇软件已经成为众多世界500强企业的重要合作伙伴，为包括宝洁、微软、IBM、GE、诺基亚、西门子、花旗银行、AVID、ADP、EA等在内的诸多知名企业提供长期服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 新宇软件是国际外包专业协会IAOP评选的&ldquo;2010年全球外包100强&rdquo;企业，及NeoIT评选的&ldquo;全球服务100强&rdquo;企业，并获得Frost &amp; Sullivan评选的&ldquo;2009中国卓越IT外包奖&rdquo;。新宇软件同时也是&ldquo;国家规划布局内重点软件企业&rdquo;、中国工信部&ldquo;中国ITO10强企业&rdquo;、 &ldquo;中国10大IT外包服务供应商第三位&rdquo;，还曾获得&ldquo;2009促进国际IT与服务外包发展最佳实践奖&rdquo;及中国评价协会&ldquo;中国服务外包最佳商业模式&rdquo; 、&ldquo;中国服务外包品牌之星&rdquo;等称号。</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">上海微创软件有限公司（外包第八名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 上海微创软件有限公司于2002年由上海市政府和美国微软公司共同投资成立，是中国领先的信息技术外包（ITO）和业务流程外包（BPO）服务提供商。公司全球共设有12处主要的运营中心，交付网络涵盖亚洲（中国、日本、新加坡、澳大利亚、新西兰、印度、中国香港地区）、北美以及欧洲的多个国家。&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 微创软件拥有自己的企业技术中心，在.net架构、无线宽带应用等方面的研究处于领先地位。至今微创已拥有27项计算机软件著作权登记证书，12项软件产品登记证书。同时，微创还建立了完备的质量管理体系，率先通过了COPC-2000、ISO9001:2008、CMM3、CMMI4、ISO27001等国际认证。</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
<span style="color:#ff0000;">深圳市易思博软件技术有限公司（外包第十名）</span></p>
<p align="left" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
深圳市易思博软件技术有限公司是中国知名的专业软件外包企业，是中国第一批从事软件外包服务的供应商。在多技术方向，多业务领域，多外包模式上积累了丰富的运作经验。</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">进入外包事业10多年来，在电信、金融、电力、IT等行业积累了丰富的经验；在网络安全、电子商务、ERP、CRM、BPO外包等领域有着专业的开发、实施和咨询能力。<br />
公司总部位于深圳, 在上海、南京、北京、广州、重庆、苏州、武汉、大连等地建立了分公司、办事处及离岸开发中心。公司拥有专业软件开发和系统实施咨询人员4000人以上，</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">高级技术人员近500人。我们提供软件研发、整体解决方案、运维及测试、BPO等服务，帮助客户聚焦于核心业务，提升全局价值。</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
<span style="color:#ff0000;">成都颠峰软件有限公司（外包第十一名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 颠峰软件集团(Sofmit)始创于2002年，总部设立在中国成都市，是一家从事软件及信息服务、业务流程外包的专业IT服务集团公司。公司以&ldquo;做您最擅长的，其余的外包&rdquo;为宗旨，不断拓展全球市场，用IT技术为客户创造价值，已经拥有了大量欧美、日本及国内成熟客户和成功案例。颠峰软件目前是商务部软件及服务外包的重点企业，科技部的欧美出口试点重点企业，中国软件外包/出口20强企业，西部最大规模的软件及服务外包公司。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &ldquo;中国服务，全球交付&rdquo;。颠峰软件在中国设立了以成都为中心的西部全球交付中心和以上海-花桥为中心的长三角全球交付中心，在美国纽约设立了Sofmit Corp.分公司，在日本东京建立了成熟稳定的运营团队，并在欧洲、东南亚等地成功进行市场拓展。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 颠峰软件通过了CMMI软件能力成熟度认证，信息安全管理ISO27001和ISO9001国际质量体系认证，以严格的服务规范流程来保障服务交付的质量、进度和成本。公司汇集了一大批立志用IT技术改变世界的优秀人才，主要管理者具有海外留学和工作背景，了解中国国情，熟悉国际企业运作和管理模式。随着公司的逐步发展和壮大，颠峰软件集团正在成为IT有志之士们创业和发展的巨大舞台。</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">联合永道（北京）信息技术有限公司（外包第十四名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 联合永道成是一家以IT服务为主的高新技术企业，主要从事软件外包、IT服务、互联网技术与应用等业务。联合永道致力于提高客户的投资回报率，为您描绘和实现能够带来商业变革的技术，提供商务和科技完美结合的解决方案 。&nbsp;<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 联合永道本着&ldquo;迅捷、诚信、尽责，打造值得信赖的国际化软件外包与服务提供商&rdquo;的愿景，面向中国市场、欧美市场、日本市场开展软件外包、IT服务、互联网技术与应用等业务。依托行业细分，联合永道向客户提供IT整体解决方案咨询与规划、应用软件开发测试、BPO、IT系统运维等服务，在多年的发展中，联合永道在政府、教育、IT行业、制造业、金融、保险、电子商务、汽车等领域积累了丰富的经验，锻炼出了一支高效的技术队伍，从而可以为全球的客户提供更加优质的支持与服务，最大可能地协助我们的客户创造价值，不断共同成长与进步！</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">武汉佰钧成技术有限责任公司（外包第十五名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 武汉佰钧成技术有限责任公司（以下简称&ldquo;佰钧成&rdquo;）正式成立于06年7月，主要业务是面向欧美、日本以及国内市场的制造业、金融、电信、能源、及IT行业提供 ITO、BPO服务。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 佰钧成现已成为IBM、Google、上海贝尔阿尔卡特、华为、NEC等近十家世界500强企业的核心供应商，并已与YRC、CBS、Honeywell、阿里巴巴、亚信等一大批知名企业结成了战略合作伙伴。<br />
凭借其丰富的大型项目管理能力以及独特的行业方案解决能力，佰钧成已成为中国中部地区领先的服务外包供应商。背靠武汉地区丰富的人才优势及良好的技术研发能力，佰钧成计划在2014年的人员规模将突破10000人。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 此外，佰钧成作为武汉服务外包协会（简称WSOA）的理事单位，在协会内领导建立了完善的人才共享机制与人才培养模式，在帮助企业汇聚区域优势的同时，有效解决了单个企业成长中遇到的人才、市场、成本等问题，为带动武汉地区软件外包服务行业的整体发展水平起到了积极的推动作用！<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 佰钧成，以&ldquo;服务全球，交付信任&rdquo;为价值理念，以不断创新为生命力，立足中部优势，不断优化资源配置，持续提升其在产业价值链的地位和作用，致力于成为全球卓越的软件外包服务商！</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">大连华信计算机技术股份有限公司（出口第二名、外包第七名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 大连华信计算机技术股份有限公司（简称大连华信）成立于1996年，专门从事计算机应用软件开发、系统集成、软件外包服务、BPO服务、ITO服务及IT教育与培训等业务。公司注册资本金1.5亿元人民币，其外资股东为NEC、NTT DATA、日立软件、NEC软件、微软、新日铁系统集成株式会社等世界知名IT企业。公司拥有员工近4000人。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 大连华信作为国内较早进入日本市场的软件企业之一，在对日软件外包服务业务领域取得了长足的发展，并与众多日本知名企业建立了良好的合作关系，在日本信息服务业排名前二十位的公司中，有十家公司与大连华信建立长期合作关系。大连华信的国际业务还涉及欧美的英国、美国、意大利和中亚的乌兹别克斯坦、南亚的孟加拉等国家，其中在中南亚国家实现了完全享有自主知识产权的软件出口。</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">海辉软件（国际）集团（出口第三名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 海辉软件（国际）集团公司成立于 1996 年，是一家一流的全球 IT 外包服务提供商，在中国、日本、美国、新加坡和墨西哥均设有办公机构。海辉拥有超过3000名专业人士的人力资源和成熟、可靠的全球交付平台，为财富 500 客户提供高质、安全的 IT 服务。作为中国首家获得 CMM Level 5 认证和 6-Sigma、ISO 27001、ISO 9001:2000 认证的 ITO 公司，海辉致力于为客户提供高质、高安全性标准的服务。海辉通过其在岸－离岸模式为美国、日本、欧洲客户提供始终如一的服务，并在 IAOP 的全球外包 100 强评选中进入前 20 名，在中国企业中排名第一。海辉关注人力资源的发展，拥有一批成功进行新老交接并经过严格培训的专业人士，为客户提供涵盖整个应用服务生命周期的服务，主要业务包括企业应用服务 (应用开发与维护，质量测试，嵌入式系统服务)，企业套装解决方案（Siebel解决方案及支持，Oracle ERP 解决方案及支持服务）、产品工程服务（产品开发和测试，产品全球化化服务），以及技术和解决方案服务（技术资源服务）。</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">浙大网新科技股份有限公司（出口第四名、外包第二名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 浙大网新科技股份有限公司（上证600797），是以浙江大学领先的计算机、机电、能源等综合应用学科为依托，以IT服务为主导的高科技产业集团，由浙大网新信息控股有限公司控股。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 浙大网新是国内最大的IT应用服务提供商和最主要的软件外包商之一，并在机电总包领域具有领先地位。浙大网新位居2005中国软件百强第8 名，2005中国电子信息百强排名第49名，同时在亚太高科技高成长500强、中国服务业企业500强等排名中也有很好表现。作为科技型上市企业的代表， 浙大网新是少数同时被选入上证180、上证50、沪深300统一指数样本股的企业。</p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;">&nbsp;</p>
<p align="center" style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><span style="color:#ff0000;">中软国际有限公司（出口第五名、外包第五名）</span></p>
<p style="padding-top:0px;padding-right:0px;padding-bottom:0px;padding-left:0px;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px;line-height:30px;"><br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 中软国际有限公司（中软国际）是根植中国、服务全球的IT服务提供商，致力于为遍及全球的客户提供全面的服务，打造中国智造综合平台。集团成立于2000年，总部位于北京，在全球拥有数十家分公司、办事处及研发机构，员工近6000人。集团业务涵盖以咨询为驱动的解决方案、以专业化为准则的ITO和BPO外包服务和以人才供链为导向的培训服务，包括咨询服务、软件开发、系统集成、软件测试、软件本地化、企业应用平台建设与维护、IT服务外包以及业务流程外包。<br />
凭借集团的全球分布，中软国际能够充分运用全球资源和自身领先的技术实力帮助客户应对不断快速变化的商业挑战。凭借中软国际在中国市场所拥有的独特领导地位和全球提交能力，除能为客户提供&ldquo;传统&rdquo;外包服务及信息解决方案外，还能以其国内、海外市场的互动能力帮助客户在中国或海外开拓新的业务机会。<br />
&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 中国经济的增长为全球IT领域提供了巨大的机会，依靠国际化的管理团队、深厚的行业经验、领先的技术力量以及卓越的人才基础，中软国际将继续秉承&ldquo;创造、分享，共成长&rdquo;的理念，成为全球IT伙伴实现梦想的理想桥梁。</p>
